Enrich_Go_sets <- function(gene_sets, v) {

  library(clusterProfiler)
  library(org.Hs.eg.db)
  library(dplyr)

  # -----------------------------
  # Universe (FIXED)
  # -----------------------------
  background_genes <- rownames(v$E) %>%
    sub("\\..*", "", .)

  # -----------------------------
  # GO helper
  # -----------------------------
  run_go <- function(genes) {

    genes <- unique(sub("\\..*", "", genes))

    if (length(genes) < 10) return(NULL)

    ego <- enrichGO(
      gene          = genes,
      universe      = background_genes,
      OrgDb         = org.Hs.eg.db,
      keyType       = "ENSEMBL",
      ont           = "BP",
      readable      = TRUE
    )

    if (is.null(ego)) return(NULL)

    as.data.frame(ego)
  }

  # -----------------------------
  # Run for each gene set
  # -----------------------------
  results <- lapply(gene_sets, function(df) {
    if (is.null(df) || nrow(df) == 0) return(NULL)
    run_go(df$Gene)
  })

  return(results)
}

colnames(design_int) <- make.names(colnames(design_int))

# saveRDS(dge, "data/DGE/dge_RNA_fc_NoRep.RDS")
# saveRDS(design_int, "data/DGE/design_int_RNA_fc_NoRep.RDS")
dge <- dge_RNA_fc_NoRep
design_int <- design_int_RNA_fc_NoRep
metadata <- RNA_Metadata_NoRep

# Step 1: voom first
v1 <- voom(dge, design_int, plot = TRUE)

# saveRDS(v1,"data/DGE/Species/concat/RowMeans_PerDay/v1_RMG0_PerDay_All.RDS")

# Step 2: estimate duplicate correlation on voom-transformed data
corfit <- duplicateCorrelation(v1, design_int, block = metadata$Individual)
corfit.correlation <- corfit$consensus.correlation

# Step 3: voom again including correlation
v2 <- voom(dge, design_int, plot = TRUE,
           block = metadata$Individual,
           correlation = corfit.correlation)

# Step 4: fit linear model
fit <- lmFit(v2, design_int, block = metadata$Individual, correlation = corfit.correlation)
fit <- eBayes(fit)

pal <- rainbow(length(unique(metadata$Timepoint)))
day <- metadata$Timepoint
plotDensities(v2, col = pal[as.numeric(day)], legend = FALSE)

human_idx <- metadata$Species == "H"
chimp_idx <- metadata$Species == "C"

pal <- rainbow(length(unique(metadata$Timepoint)))

# Human
plotDensities(
  v2[, human_idx],
  col = pal[as.numeric(as.factor(metadata$Timepoint[human_idx]))],
  main = "",
  legend = FALSE,
  axes = FALSE
)

axis(2)
mtext("log2 CPM", side = 1, line = 2)

  legend(
      "right",
      legend = metadata$Individual[human_idx],  # or Timepoint, etc.
      col = rainbow(sum(human_idx)),
      lty = 1,
     cex = 0.7
    )

# Chimp
plotDensities(
  v2[, chimp_idx],
  col = pal[as.numeric(as.factor(metadata$Timepoint[human_idx]))],
  main = "",
  legend = FALSE,
  axes = FALSE
)

axis(1)
axis(2)
mtext("log2 CPM", side = 1, line = 2)

title("Chimp")
  legend(
      "right",
      legend = metadata$Individual[chimp_idx],  # or Timepoint, etc.
      col = rainbow(sum(chimp_idx)),
      lty = 1,
     cex = 0.7
    )

species_levels <- unique(metadata$Species)
day_levels <- unique(metadata$Timepoint)

for (sp in species_levels) {
  for (day in day_levels) {

    idx <- metadata$Species == sp &
           metadata$Timepoint == day

    if (sum(idx) > 0) {

      cols <- rainbow(sum(idx))

      plotDensities(
        v2[, idx],
        col = cols,
        main = paste(sp, day),
        legend = FALSE,
        axes = FALSE
      )

      axis(1)
      axis(2)
      mtext("log2 CPM", side = 1, line = 2)

      legend(
        "right",
        legend = metadata$Individual[idx],
        col = cols,
        lty = 1,
        cex = 0.7
      )
    }
  }
}

metadata$Species <- factor(
  metadata$Species,
  levels = c("C", "H")   # Chimp baseline
)

 metadata$Timepoint <- factor(
   metadata$Timepoint,
  levels = c("Day0","Day2","Day4","Day5","Day15","Day30")
)

design_int <- model.matrix(~ Species * Timepoint,
                           data =  metadata)

colnames(design_int)

 [3] "TimepointDay2"           "TimepointDay4"

 [9] "SpeciesH:TimepointDay4"  "SpeciesH:TimepointDay5" 
[11] "SpeciesH:TimepointDay15" "SpeciesH:TimepointDay30"
colnames(design_int) <- make.names(colnames(design_int))

# Step 1: voom first
v1 <- voom(dge, design_int, plot = TRUE)

# Step 2: estimate duplicate correlation on voom-transformed data
corfit <- duplicateCorrelation(v1, design_int, block = metadata$Individual)
corfit.correlation <- corfit$consensus.correlation

# Step 3: voom again including correlation
v2 <- voom(dge, design_int, plot = TRUE,
           block = metadata$Individual,
           correlation = corfit.correlation)

# Step 4: fit linear model
fit <- lmFit(v2, design_int, block = metadata$Individual, correlation = corfit.correlation)
fit <- eBayes(fit)

pal <- rainbow(length(unique(metadata$Timepoint)))
day <- metadata$Timepoint

for (sp in species_levels) {
  for (day in day_levels) {

    idx <- metadata$Species == sp &
           metadata$Timepoint == day

    if (sum(idx) > 0) {

      cols <- rainbow(sum(idx))

      plotDensities(
        v2[, idx],
        col = cols,

# saveRDS(dge, "data/DGE/dge_Filt_logcpm_G1_SpTp_RNA_fc_NoRep.RDS")
# saveRDS(design_int, "data/DGE/design_Filt_logcpm_G1_SpTp_RNA_fc_NoRep.RDS")
# saveRDS(v1,"data/DGE/v1_Filt_logcpm_G1_SpTp_RNA_fc_NoRep.RDS")
# saveRDS(fit, "data/DGE/fit_Filt_logcpm_G1_SpTp_RNA_fc_NoRep.RDS")
fit <- fit_Filt_logcpm_G1_SpTp_RNA_fc_NoRep
design_int <- design_Filt_logcpm_G1_SpTp_RNA_fc_NoRep

contrast_matrix <- makeContrasts(

  # Species differences
  HvC_Day0  = SpeciesH,
  HvC_Day2  = SpeciesH + SpeciesH.TimepointDay2,
  HvC_Day4  = SpeciesH + SpeciesH.TimepointDay4,
  HvC_Day5  = SpeciesH + SpeciesH.TimepointDay5,
  HvC_Day15 = SpeciesH + SpeciesH.TimepointDay15,
  HvC_Day30 = SpeciesH + SpeciesH.TimepointDay30,
  
  #Trajectory differences
  H_Day02 = TimepointDay2 + SpeciesH.TimepointDay2,
  H_Day24 = TimepointDay4 + SpeciesH.TimepointDay4 - TimepointDay2 - SpeciesH.TimepointDay2,
  H_Day45 = TimepointDay5 + SpeciesH.TimepointDay5 - TimepointDay4 - SpeciesH.TimepointDay4,
  H_Day515 = TimepointDay15 + SpeciesH.TimepointDay15 - TimepointDay5 - SpeciesH.TimepointDay5,
  H_Day1530 = TimepointDay30 + SpeciesH.TimepointDay30 - TimepointDay15 - SpeciesH.TimepointDay15,
  C_Day02 = TimepointDay2,
  C_Day24 = TimepointDay4 - TimepointDay2,
  C_Day45 = TimepointDay5 - TimepointDay4,
  C_Day515 = TimepointDay15 - TimepointDay5,
  C_Day1530 = TimepointDay30 - TimepointDay15,
  
  # True interaction tests trajectory
  Sig_Sp_inter_Traj02 = SpeciesH.TimepointDay2,
  Sig_Sp_inter_Traj24 = SpeciesH.TimepointDay4 - SpeciesH.TimepointDay2,
  Sig_Sp_inter_Traj45 = SpeciesH.TimepointDay5 - SpeciesH.TimepointDay4,
  Sig_Sp_inter_Traj515 = SpeciesH.TimepointDay15 - SpeciesH.TimepointDay5,
  Sig_Sp_inter_Traj1530 = SpeciesH.TimepointDay30 - SpeciesH.TimepointDay15,
  
  levels = design_int
)

fit2 <- contrasts.fit(fit, contrast_matrix)
fit2 <- eBayes(fit2)

plotSA(fit2, main = "RNA Model")

results_summary <- decideTests(fit2,
                               adjust.method = "BH",
                               p.value = 0.05)
summary(results_summary)

# saveRDS(fit2, "data/DGE/fit2_Filt_logcpm_G1_SpTp_RNA_fc_NoRep.RDS")
fit2 <- fit2_Filt_logcpm_G1_SpTp_RNA_fc_NoRep

#Create Human TopTable. using listapply, then you can pull specific comp using the $
TopTables_RNA_names <- colnames(fit2$coefficients) 

TopTable_RNA_All <- do.call(
  rbind,
  lapply(TopTables_RNA_names,function(ct) {
    
    tt <- topTable(
      fit2,
      coef = ct,
      number = Inf,
      sort.by = "p"
    )
    
    #add identifiers
    tt$Gene <- rownames(tt)
    tt$Comparisons <- ct
    
    tt
  })
)

ComparisonNames <- unique(TopTable_RNA_All$Comparisons)

# Calculate global axis limits
x_limits <- range(TopTable$logFC, na.rm = TRUE)
y_limits <- range(-log10(TopTable$P.Value), na.rm = TRUE)

plot <- list()

for (n in ComparisonNames) {
  data_n <- TopTable %>% 
    dplyr::filter(Comparisons == n)
  
  plot[[n]] <- generate_volcano_plot(data_n, n) +
    ggplot2::xlim(x_limits) +
    ggplot2::ylim(y_limits)
}

# Print plots
for (n in ComparisonNames) {
  print(plot[[n]])
}

RNA_sets <- map(
  ComparisonNames,
  ~ {
    df <- TopTable %>%
      filter(Comparisons == paste0(.x))

    list(
      DEGs = df %>% filter(adj.P.Val < 0.05),
      NonDEGs = df %>% filter(adj.P.Val >= 0.05)
    )
  }
)

TopTable <- TopTable_Filt_logcpm_G1_SpTp_RNA_fc_NoRep

traj_info <- list(
  Traj02_genes = list(coef = "H_Day02", comp = "Day02"),
  Traj24_genes = list(coef = "H_Day24", comp = "Day24"),
  Traj45_genes = list(coef = "H_Day45", comp = "Day45"),
  Traj515_genes = list(coef ="H_Day515", comp = "Day515"),
 Traj1530_genes = list(coef = "H_Day1530", comp = "Day1530")
)

direction_results <- setNames(
  lapply(names(traj_info), function(name) {

    info <- traj_info[[name]]

    get_fc_directions(
      traj_label = name,
      coef_name = info$coef,
      comparison_label = info$comp,
      top_table_all = TopTable,
      fit_obj = fit2,
      gene_set = cluster_lists[[name]]
    )

  }),
  names(traj_info)
)

ComparisonNames <- ComparisonNames_Filt_logcpm_G1_SpTp_RNA_fc_NoRep
direction_results <- Trajectory_Directions_Filt_logcpm_G1_SpTp_RNA_fc_NoR

TopTable$absfc <- abs(TopTable$logFC)

TopTable_Traj <- TopTable %>% 
  filter(Comparisons %in% c(
    "H_Day02","H_Day24","H_Day45","H_Day515","H_Day1530",
    "C_Day02","C_Day24","C_Day45","C_Day515","C_Day1530"
  ))

TopTable <- TopTable_Filt_logcpm_G1_SpTp_RNA_fc_NoRep
RNA_sets <- RNA_sets_Filt_logcpm_G1_SpTp_RNA_fc_NoRep


H_comp <- "H_Day02"
C_comp <- "C_Day02"

df_wide <- TopTable %>%
  filter(Comparisons %in% c(H_comp, C_comp)) %>%
  dplyr::select(Gene, Comparisons, logFC) %>%
  group_by(Gene, Comparisons) %>%
  summarize(logFC = mean(logFC), .groups = "drop") %>%
  pivot_wider(names_from = Comparisons, values_from = logFC) %>%
  filter(!is.na(.data[[H_comp]]), !is.na(.data[[C_comp]]))

# head(df_wide)
# nrow(df_wide)

fit <- lm(df_wide[[C_comp]] ~ df_wide[[H_comp]])
summary(fit)

Call:
lm(formula = df_wide[[C_comp]] ~ df_wide[[H_comp]])

Residuals:
    Min      1Q  Median      3Q     Max

                  Estimate Std. Error t value Pr(>|t|)

df_wide[[H_comp]] 0.721981   0.005311  135.94   <2e-16 ***

Residual standard error: 0.9032 on 15866 degrees of freedom
Multiple R-squared:  0.538, Adjusted R-squared:  0.538 
F-statistic: 1.848e+04 on 1 and 15866 DF,  p-value: < 2.2e-16
r2 <- summary(fit)$r.squared
pval <- summary(fit)$coefficients[2, "Pr(>|t|)"]

library(ggplot2)

x_pos <- max(df_wide[[H_comp]]) * 0.95      # right side
x_neg <- min(df_wide[[H_comp]]) * 0.5      # left side

y_pos <- max(df_wide[[C_comp]]) * 0.95

# Optional: make axes symmetric around 0 for a nicer visual
max_val <- max(abs(c(x_limits, y_limits)))
x_limits <- c(-15, 15)
y_limits <- c(-15, 15)


genes_of_interest_human <- unique(RNA_sets$H_Day02$DEGs$Gene)
genes_of_interest_chimp <- unique(RNA_sets$C_Day02$DEGs$Gene)

df_wide$highlight <- dplyr::case_when(
  df_wide$Gene %in% genes_of_interest_human &
  df_wide$Gene %in% genes_of_interest_chimp ~ "T-DEG Both",

  df_wide$Gene %in% genes_of_interest_human ~ "T-DEG Human Only",

  df_wide$Gene %in% genes_of_interest_chimp ~ "T-DEG Chimp Only",

  TRUE ~ "Other"
)

# Plot
ggplot(df_wide, aes(x = .data[[H_comp]], y = .data[[C_comp]], color = highlight)) +
  geom_point(size = 3, alpha = 0.8) +
  scale_color_manual(values = c("T-DEG Human Only" = "red", "T-DEG Chimp Only" = "blue", "T-DEG Both" = "purple", "Other" = "grey70")) +
  geom_smooth(method = "lm", se = FALSE, linetype = "dashed", color = "black") +
  geom_hline(yintercept = 0, linetype = "dashed") +
  geom_vline(xintercept = 0, linetype = "dashed") +
  annotate(
    "text",
    x = min(df_wide[[H_comp]], na.rm = TRUE),
    y = max(df_wide[[C_comp]], na.rm = TRUE),
    label = paste0(
      "R² = ", round(r2, 3),
      "\np = ", format(pval, scientific = TRUE, digits = 3)
    ),
    hjust = 0,
    vjust = 1
  ) +
  coord_cartesian(xlim = x_limits, ylim = y_limits) +
  theme_bw() +
  labs(
    x = H_comp,
    y = C_comp,
    title = paste0(H_comp, " vs ", C_comp),
    color = "Gene Set"
  )

  scale_color_manual(values = c("T-DEG Human Only" = "red", "T-DEG Chimp Only" = "blue", "T-DEG Both" = "purple", "Other" = "grey70")) +
  geom_smooth(method = "lm", se = FALSE, linetype = "dashed", color = "black") +
  geom_hline(yintercept = 0, linetype = "dashed") +
  geom_vline(xintercept = 0, linetype = "dashed") +
  annotate(
    "text",
    x = min(df_wide[[H_comp]], na.rm = TRUE),
    y = max(df_wide[[C_comp]], na.rm = TRUE),
    label = paste0(
      "R² = ", round(r2, 3),
      "\np = ", format(pval, scientific = TRUE, digits = 3)
    ),
    hjust = 0,
    vjust = 1
  ) +
  coord_cartesian(xlim = x_limits, ylim = y_limits) +
  theme_bw() +
  labs(
    x = H_comp,
    y = C_comp,
    title = paste0(H_comp, " vs ", C_comp),
    color = "Gene Set"
  )

TopTable <- TopTable_Filt_logcpm_G1_SpTp_RNA_fc_NoRep
RNA_sets <- RNA_sets_Filt_logcpm_G1_SpTp_RNA_fc_NoRep

library(dplyr)
library(tidyr)
library(stringr)

df_all <- TopTable %>%
  dplyr::select(Gene, Comparisons, logFC) %>%
  
  mutate(
    species = ifelse(str_starts(Comparisons, "H_"), "H", "C"),
    trajectory = str_remove(Comparisons, "^[HC]_")
  ) %>%
  
  group_by(Gene, species, trajectory) %>%
  summarize(logFC = mean(logFC), .groups = "drop") %>%
  
  pivot_wider(names_from = species, values_from = logFC) %>%
  
  filter(!is.na(H), !is.na(C))

library(ggplot2)

df_all$trajectory <- df_all$trajectory <- factor(
  df_all$trajectory,
  levels = c("Day02", "Day24", "Day45", "Day515","Day1530")
)

ggplot(df_all, aes(x = H, y = C, color = trajectory)) +
  geom_point(alpha = 0.7) +
  
  # one regression line per trajectory (same color as points)
  geom_smooth(method = "lm", se = FALSE, fullrange = TRUE)+
  
  geom_hline(yintercept = 0, linetype = "dashed") +
  geom_vline(xintercept = 0, linetype = "dashed") +
  
  theme_bw() +
  labs(
    x = "Human logFC",
    y = "Chimp logFC",
    color = "Trajectory",
    title = "All Trajectories Combined"
  )

df_stats <- df_all %>%
  group_by(trajectory) %>%
  do({
    fit <- lm(C ~ H, data = .)
    data.frame(
      r2 = summary(fit)$r.squared,
      p = summary(fit)$coefficients[2, "Pr(>|t|)"]
    )
  })

metadata$Species <- factor(
  metadata$Species,
  levels = c("C", "H")   # Chimp baseline
)

 metadata$Timepoint <- factor(
   metadata$Timepoint,
  levels = c("Day0","Day2","Day5","Day15","Day30")
)

design_int <- model.matrix(~ Species * Timepoint,
                           data =  metadata)

colnames(design_int)

species_levels <- unique(metadata$Species)
day_levels <- unique(metadata$Timepoint)

for (sp in species_levels) {
  for (day in day_levels) {

    idx <- metadata$Species == sp &
           metadata$Timepoint == day

    if (sum(idx) > 0) {

      cols <- rainbow(sum(idx))

      plotDensities(
        v2[, idx],
        col = cols,
        main = paste(sp, day),
        legend = FALSE,
        axes = FALSE
      )

      axis(1)
      axis(2)
      mtext("log2 CPM", side = 1, line = 2)

      legend(
        "right",
        legend = metadata$Individual[idx],
        col = cols,
        lty = 1,
        cex = 0.7
      )
    }
  }
}

fit <- fit_Filt_logcpm_G1_SpTp_RNA_fc_NoRep_No4
design_int <- design_Filt_logcpm_G1_SpTp_RNA_fc_NoRep_No4


contrast_matrix <- makeContrasts(

  # Species differences
  HvC_Day0  = SpeciesH,
  HvC_Day2  = SpeciesH + SpeciesH.TimepointDay2,
  HvC_Day5  = SpeciesH + SpeciesH.TimepointDay5,
  HvC_Day15 = SpeciesH + SpeciesH.TimepointDay15,
  HvC_Day30 = SpeciesH + SpeciesH.TimepointDay30,
  
  #Trajectory differences
  H_Day02 = TimepointDay2 + SpeciesH.TimepointDay2,
  H_Day25 = TimepointDay5 + SpeciesH.TimepointDay5 - TimepointDay2 - SpeciesH.TimepointDay2,
  H_Day515 = TimepointDay15 + SpeciesH.TimepointDay15 - TimepointDay5 - SpeciesH.TimepointDay5,
  H_Day1530 = TimepointDay30 + SpeciesH.TimepointDay30 - TimepointDay15 - SpeciesH.TimepointDay15,
  C_Day02 = TimepointDay2,
  C_Day25 = TimepointDay5 - TimepointDay2,
  C_Day515 = TimepointDay15 - TimepointDay5,
  C_Day1530 = TimepointDay30 - TimepointDay15,
  
  # True interaction tests trajectory
  Sig_Sp_inter_Traj02 = SpeciesH.TimepointDay2,
  Sig_Sp_inter_Traj25 = SpeciesH.TimepointDay5 - SpeciesH.TimepointDay2,
  Sig_Sp_inter_Traj515 = SpeciesH.TimepointDay15 - SpeciesH.TimepointDay5,
  Sig_Sp_inter_Traj1530 = SpeciesH.TimepointDay30 - SpeciesH.TimepointDay15,
  
  levels = design_int
)

fit2 <- contrasts.fit(fit, contrast_matrix)
fit2 <- eBayes(fit2)

plotSA(fit2, main = "RNA Model")

                               adjust.method = "BH",
                               p.value = 0.05)

# saveRDS(fit2, "data/DGE/fit2_Filt_logcpm_G1_SpTp_RNA_fc_NoRep_No4.RDS")
fit2 <- fit2_Filt_logcpm_G1_SpTp_RNA_fc_NoRep_No4

#Create Human TopTable. using listapply, then you can pull specific comp using the $
TopTables_RNA_names <- colnames(fit2$coefficients) 

TopTable_RNA_All <- do.call(
  rbind,
  lapply(TopTables_RNA_names,function(ct) {
    
    tt <- topTable(
      fit2,
      coef = ct,
      number = Inf,
      sort.by = "p"
    )
    
    #add identifiers
    tt$Gene <- rownames(tt)
    tt$Comparisons <- ct
    
    tt
  })
)

ComparisonNames <- unique(TopTable_RNA_All$Comparisons)

# saveRDS(TopTable_RNA_All, "data/DGE/TopTable_Filt_logcpm_G1_SpTp_RNA_fc_NoRep_No4.RDS")
# saveRDS(ComparisonNames, "data/DGE/ComparisonNames_Filt_logcpm_G1_SpTp_RNA_fc_NoRep_No4.RDS")

ComparisonNames <- ComparisonNames_Filt_logcpm_G1_SpTp_RNA_fc_NoRep_No4

# Calculate global axis limits
x_limits <- range(TopTable$logFC, na.rm = TRUE)
y_limits <- range(-log10(TopTable$P.Value), na.rm = TRUE)

plot <- list()

for (n in ComparisonNames) {
  data_n <- TopTable %>% 
    dplyr::filter(Comparisons == n)
  
  plot[[n]] <- generate_volcano_plot(data_n, n) +
    ggplot2::xlim(x_limits) +
    ggplot2::ylim(y_limits)
}

# Print plots
for (n in ComparisonNames) {
  print(plot[[n]])
}

TopTable <- TopTable_Filt_logcpm_G1_SpTp_RNA_fc_NoRep_No4
ComparisonNames <- ComparisonNames_Filt_logcpm_G1_SpTp_RNA_fc_NoRep_No4

RNA_sets <- map(
  ComparisonNames,
  ~ {
    df <- TopTable %>%
      filter(Comparisons == paste0(.x))

    list(
      DEGs = df %>% filter(adj.P.Val < 0.05),
      NonDEGs = df %>% filter(adj.P.Val >= 0.05)
    )
  }
)


names(RNA_sets) <- paste0(ComparisonNames)

Species_go_results_Filt_logcpm_G1_SpTp_RNA_fc_NoRep_No4 <-readRDS("data/DGE/Species_go_results_Filt_logcpm_G1_SpTp_RNA_fc_NoRep_No4.RDS")
library(dplyr)
library(purrr)
library(stringr)

hvcdays <- names(RNA_sets)[str_detect(names(RNA_sets), "^HvC_")]

prop_df <- map_dfr(hvcdays, function(traj) {
  
  x <- RNA_sets[[traj]]
  
  tibble(
    trajectory = traj,
    DEG = length(x$DEGs$Gene),
    NonDEG = length(x$NonDEGs$Gene)
  )
})
library(tidyr)

prop_long <- prop_df %>%
  pivot_longer(cols = c(DEG, NonDEG),
               names_to = "type",
               values_to = "count") %>%
  group_by(trajectory) %>%
  mutate(prop = count / sum(count)) %>%
  ungroup()
prop_long$trajectory <- factor(
  prop_long$trajectory,
  levels = c("HvC_Day0", "HvC_Day2", "HvC_Day5", "HvC_Day15", "HvC_Day30"),
  labels = c("0", "2", "5", "15", "30")
)
library(ggplot2)

ggplot(prop_long, aes(x = trajectory, y = prop, fill = type)) +
  geom_col() +
  theme_bw() +
  labs(
    x = "Time",
    y = "Proportion of genes",
    fill = "",
    title = "HvC comparisons: DEG vs NonDEG composition"
  )

library(dplyr)
library(stringr)

df <- TopTable %>%
  filter(str_detect(Comparisons, "^HvC_Day")) %>%
  mutate(
    Stage = str_extract(Comparisons, "Day[0-9]+"),
    DEG = adj.P.Val < 0.05
  ) %>%
  filter(DEG)

genes <- list(
  Day0  = df %>% filter(Stage == "Day0")  %>% pull(Gene) %>% unique(),
  Day2  = df %>% filter(Stage == "Day2")  %>% pull(Gene) %>% unique(),
  Day5  = df %>% filter(Stage == "Day5")  %>% pull(Gene) %>% unique(),
  Day15 = df %>% filter(Stage == "Day15") %>% pull(Gene) %>% unique(),
  Day30 = df %>% filter(Stage == "Day30") %>% pull(Gene) %>% unique()
)

days <- names(genes)

shared_all <- Reduce(intersect, genes)

get_fate <- function(day) {

  g <- genes[[day]]

  specific <- setdiff(g, unlist(genes[names(genes) != day]))

  shared_all_day <- intersect(g, shared_all)

  shared_partial <- setdiff(
    setdiff(g, specific),
    shared_all_day
  )

  data.frame(
    Day = day,
    Specific = length(specific),
    Shared_partial = length(shared_partial),
    Shared_all = length(shared_all_day)
  )
}

plot_df <- do.call(rbind, lapply(names(genes), get_fate))

library(tidyr)

plot_long <- plot_df %>%
  pivot_longer(
    cols = c(Specific, Shared_partial, Shared_all),
    names_to = "Category",
    values_to = "Count"
  )

plot_long$Day <- factor(
  plot_long$Day,
  levels = c("Day0","Day2","Day5","Day15","Day30")
)

library(ggplot2)

ggplot(plot_long, aes(x = Day, y = Count, fill = Category)) +
  geom_col() +
  theme_bw() +
  labs(
    x = "Developmental stage",
    y = "Number of DEGs",
    fill = "",
    title = "Fate of HvC DEGs across development"
  )

library(dplyr)
library(tidyr)

plot_long_prop <- plot_df %>%
  pivot_longer(
    cols = c(Specific, Shared_partial, Shared_all),
    names_to = "Category",
    values_to = "Count"
  ) %>%
  group_by(Day) %>%
  mutate(
    Prop = Count / sum(Count)
  ) %>%
  ungroup()

plot_long_prop$Day <- factor(
  plot_long_prop$Day,
  levels = c("Day0","Day2","Day5","Day15","Day30")
)
library(ggplot2)

ggplot(plot_long_prop, aes(x = Day, y = Prop, fill = Category)) +
  geom_col() +
  
  scale_fill_manual(values = c(
    "Specific" = "#D55E00",
    "Shared_partial" = "#0072B2",
    "Shared_all" = "#009E73"
  )) +
  
  theme_bw() +
  labs(
    x = "Developmental stage",
    y = "Proportion of DEGs",
    fill = "",
    title = "Fate of HvC DEGs across development (normalized)"
  )

# saveRDS(all_go_results, "data/DGE/Trajectory_go_results_Filt_logcpm_G1_SpTp_RNA_fc_NoRep_No4.RDS")
Trajectory_go_results_Filt_logcpm_G1_SpTp_RNA_fc_NoRep_No4 <- readRDS("data/DGE/Trajectory_go_results_Filt_logcpm_G1_SpTp_RNA_fc_NoRep_No4.RDS")
all_go_results <- Trajectory_go_results_Filt_logcpm_G1_SpTp_RNA_fc_NoRep_No4

go_all <- imap_dfr(all_go_results, function(x, name) {

  df <- x$Same_direction
  if (is.null(df)) return(NULL)

  df %>%
    mutate(trajectory = name)
})

go_all <- go_all %>%
  mutate(trajectory = recode(
    trajectory,
    "Traj02_genes"   = "Day02",
    "Traj25_genes"   = "Day25",
    "Traj515_genes"  = "Day5-15",
    "Traj1530_genes" = "Day15-30"
  ))

is_dev <- function(x) {
  grepl("development|morphogenesis|differentiation", x, ignore.case = TRUE)
}

go_summary <- go_all %>%
  mutate(dev = is_dev(Description)) %>%
  group_by(trajectory) %>%
  summarise(
    prop_dev = mean(dev),
    n_terms = n(),
    .groups = "drop"
  )

library(ggplot2)

ggplot(go_summary, aes(x = trajectory, y = prop_dev)) +
  geom_col(fill = "black") +
  theme_bw() +
  labs(
    x = "Trajectory",
    y = "Proportion developmental GO terms",
    title = "GO enrichment of DEGs (All)"
  )

library(dplyr)

traj <- c(
  "H_Day02","H_Day25","H_Day515","H_Day1530",
  "C_Day02","C_Day25","C_Day515","C_Day1530"
)

# 1. Filter + define DEG status
df <- TopTable %>%
  filter(Comparisons %in% traj) %>%
  mutate(DEG_status = ifelse(adj.P.Val < 0.05, "DEG", "Non-DEG"))

# 2. Summarise proportions per comparison
prop_df <- df %>%
  group_by(Comparisons, DEG_status) %>%
  summarise(n = n(), .groups = "drop") %>%
  group_by(Comparisons) %>%
  mutate(prop = n / sum(n)) %>%
  ungroup()

# 3. Order comparisons properly
prop_df$Comparisons <- factor(
  prop_df$Comparisons,
  levels = c(
    "H_Day02","H_Day25","H_Day515","H_Day1530",
    "C_Day02","C_Day25","C_Day515","C_Day1530"
  )
)

# 4. Plot
library(ggplot2)

ggplot(prop_df, aes(x = Comparisons, y = prop, fill = DEG_status)) +
  geom_col() +
  theme_bw() +
  labs(
    x = "Time",
    y = "Proportion of genes",
    fill = "",
    title = "DEG vs NonDEG composition"
  )

  dplyr::mutate(
    Species = ifelse(grepl("^H", Comparisons), "Human", "Chimp"),

  group_by(Gene, Stage, Species) %>%
  summarise(.groups = "drop")

  tidyr::pivot_wider(
    names_from = Species,
    values_from = Gene,
    values_fn = length,
    values_fill = 0
  )

df_flags <- df_deg2 %>%
  mutate(flag = TRUE) %>%
  tidyr::pivot_wider(
    names_from = Species,
    values_from = flag,
    values_fill = FALSE
  ) %>%
  dplyr::mutate(
    category = case_when(
      Human & Chimp ~ "Shared",
      Human ~ "Human only",
      Chimp ~ "Chimp only"
    )
  )

plot_df <- df_flags %>%
  group_by(Stage, category) %>%
  summarise(n = n(), .groups = "drop") %>%
  group_by(Stage) %>%
  mutate(prop = n / sum(n))

  plot_df$Stage,
  levels = c("Day02", "Day25", "Day515", "Day1530")
)

# ----------------------------
# 1. Define trajectories
# ----------------------------
traj <- c(
  "H_Day02","H_Day25","H_Day515","H_Day1530",
  "C_Day02","C_Day25","C_Day515","C_Day1530"
)

# ----------------------------
# 2. Prepare long data
# ----------------------------
df <- TopTable %>%
  filter(Comparisons %in% traj) %>%
  mutate(
    Species = ifelse(str_detect(Comparisons, "^H"), "Human", "Chimp"),
    Stage = str_extract(Comparisons, "Day[0-9]+"),
    DEG = adj.P.Val < 0.05
  )

# ----------------------------
# 3. Collapse to gene-level (keep all DEGs in either species)
# ----------------------------
df_wide <- df %>%
  dplyr::select(Gene, Species, Stage, logFC, DEG) %>%
  pivot_wider(
    names_from = Species,
    values_from = c(logFC, DEG)
  )

df_deg <- df_wide %>%
  filter(DEG_Human | DEG_Chimp)   # ALL DEGs (union)

# ----------------------------
# 4. Build plotting dataset
# ----------------------------
plot_df <- df_deg %>%
  mutate(
    logFC_H = abs(logFC_Human),
    logFC_C = abs(logFC_Chimp)
  ) %>%
  dplyr::select(Gene, Stage, logFC_H, logFC_C) %>%
  pivot_longer(
    cols = c(logFC_H, logFC_C),
    names_to = "Species",
    values_to = "abs_logFC"
  ) %>%
  mutate(
    Species = ifelse(Species == "logFC_H", "Human", "Chimp"),
    Stage = factor(Stage, levels = c("Day02","Day25","Day515","Day1530"))
  )

# ----------------------------
# 5. Plot
# ----------------------------
ggplot(plot_df, aes(x = Species, y = abs_logFC, fill = Species)) +
  geom_boxplot() +
  facet_wrap(~Stage, nrow = 1) +
  scale_fill_manual(values = c(
    "Human" = "black",
    "Chimp" = "white"
  )) +
  coord_cartesian(ylim = c(0, 2)) +
  theme_bw() +
  labs(
    x = "",
    y = "|logFC| (all DEGs)",
    title = "Effect sizes across all DEGs"
  )

library(dplyr)
library(stringr)
library(tidyr)
library(ggplot2)

# ----------------------------
# 1. Define trajectories
# ----------------------------
traj <- c(
  "H_Day02","H_Day25","H_Day515","H_Day1530",
  "C_Day02","C_Day25","C_Day515","C_Day1530"
)

# ----------------------------
# 2. Prepare long data
# ----------------------------
df <- TopTable %>%
  filter(Comparisons %in% traj) %>%
  mutate(
    Species = ifelse(str_detect(Comparisons, "^H"), "Human", "Chimp"),
    Stage = str_extract(Comparisons, "Day[0-9]+"),
    DEG = adj.P.Val < 0.05
  )

# ----------------------------
# 3. Collapse to gene-level
# ----------------------------
df_wide <- df %>%
  dplyr::select(Gene, Species, Stage, logFC, DEG) %>%
  pivot_wider(
    names_from = Species,
    values_from = c(logFC, DEG)
  )

# ----------------------------
# 4. Build species-specific DEG sets
# ----------------------------
plot_df <- df_wide %>%
  mutate(
    use_H = DEG_Human,   # Human uses its DEGs (shared + human-only)
    use_C = DEG_Chimp    # Chimp uses its DEGs (shared + chimp-only)
  ) %>%
  dplyr::select(Gene, Stage,
         logFC_Human, logFC_Chimp,
         use_H, use_C) %>%
  
  # reshape manually into long format
  pivot_longer(
    cols = c(logFC_Human, logFC_Chimp),
    names_to = "Species",
    values_to = "logFC"
  ) %>%
  
  mutate(
    use = ifelse(
      Species == "logFC_Human", use_H,
      use_C
    ),
    Species = ifelse(Species == "logFC_Human", "Human", "Chimp")
  ) %>%
  
  filter(use) %>%   # keep only DEGs for that species
  
  mutate(
    abs_logFC = abs(logFC),
    Stage = factor(Stage, levels = c("Day02","Day25","Day515","Day1530"))
  )

# ----------------------------
# 5. Plot
# ----------------------------
ggplot(plot_df, aes(x = Species, y = abs_logFC, fill = Species)) +
  geom_boxplot() +
  facet_wrap(~Stage, nrow = 1) +
  scale_fill_manual(values = c(
    "Human" = "black",
    "Chimp" = "white"
  )) +
  coord_cartesian(ylim = c(0, 3)) +
  theme_bw() +
  labs(
    x = "",
    y = "|logFC| (species-specific DEGs)",
    title = "Effect sizes within each species' DEG set"
  )

# 2. Prepare long data
# ----------------------------
df <- TopTable %>%
  filter(Comparisons %in% traj) %>%
  mutate(
    Species = ifelse(str_detect(Comparisons, "^H"), "Human", "Chimp"),
    Stage = str_extract(Comparisons, "Day[0-9]+"),
    DEG = adj.P.Val < 0.05
  )

# ----------------------------
# 3. Pair Human and Chimp values
# ----------------------------
df_wide <- df %>%
  dplyr::select(Gene, Species, Stage, logFC, DEG) %>%
  pivot_wider(
    names_from = Species,
    values_from = c(logFC, DEG)
  )

# ----------------------------
# 4. KEEP ALL DEGs (union)
# ----------------------------
df_deg <- df_wide %>%
  filter(DEG_Human | DEG_Chimp)

# ----------------------------
# 5. Compute divergence
# ----------------------------
plot_df <- df_deg %>%
  mutate(
    diff_logFC = abs(logFC_Human - logFC_Chimp),
    Stage = factor(Stage, levels = c("Day02","Day25","Day515","Day1530"))
  )

# ----------------------------
# 6. Plot
# ----------------------------

  geom_boxplot(fill = "grey80", color = "black") +
  geom_hline(yintercept = 0, linetype = "dashed") +
  coord_cartesian(ylim = c(0, 2)) +
  theme_bw() +
  labs(
    x = "Developmental Stage",
    y = "|H logFC − C logFC|",
    title = "Species divergence across all DEGs"
  )

df_stats <- df_all %>%
  group_by(trajectory) %>%
  do({
    fit <- lm(C ~ H, data = .)
    data.frame(
      r2 = round(summary(fit)$r.squared, 3),
      p = format(summary(fit)$coefficients[2, "Pr(>|t|)"], scientific = TRUE, digits = 2)
    )
  })

  geom_text(
    data = df_stats,
    aes(
      x = -Inf, y = Inf,
      label = paste0("R² = ", r2, "\np = ", p)
    ),
    hjust = -0.1,
    vjust = 1.1,

library(dplyr)
library(stringr)
library(tidyr)
library(ggplot2)

# ----------------------------
# 1. Define trajectories
# ----------------------------
traj <- c(
  "H_Day02","H_Day25","H_Day515","H_Day1530",
  "C_Day02","C_Day25","C_Day515","C_Day1530"
)

# ----------------------------
# 2. Prepare long data
# ----------------------------
df <- TopTable %>%
  filter(Comparisons %in% traj) %>%
  mutate(
    Species = ifelse(str_detect(Comparisons, "^H"), "Human", "Chimp"),
    trajectory = str_extract(Comparisons, "Day[0-9]+"),
    DEG = adj.P.Val < 0.05
  )

# ----------------------------
# 3. Pivot to paired H vs C
# ----------------------------
df_wide <- df %>%
  dplyr::select(Gene, Species, trajectory, logFC, DEG) %>%
  pivot_wider(
    names_from = Species,
    values_from = c(logFC, DEG)
  )

# ----------------------------
# 4. KEEP ONLY shared DEGs
# ----------------------------
df_all <- df_wide %>%
  filter(DEG_Human & DEG_Chimp)

# ----------------------------
# 5. Format for plotting
# ----------------------------
df_all <- df_all %>%
  mutate(
    H = logFC_Human,
    C = logFC_Chimp,
    trajectory = factor(
      trajectory,
      levels = c("Day02","Day25","Day515","Day1530"),
      labels = c("Day0-Day2","Day2-Day5","Day5-Day15","Day15-Day30")
    )
  )

# ----------------------------
# 6. Scatter plots + regression
# ----------------------------
ggplot(df_all, aes(x = H, y = C, color = trajectory)) +
  geom_point(alpha = 0.7) +
  geom_smooth(method = "lm", se = FALSE, fullrange = TRUE) +
  geom_hline(yintercept = 0, linetype = "dashed") +
  geom_vline(xintercept = 0, linetype = "dashed") +
  facet_wrap(~ trajectory, ncol = 2) +
  theme_bw() +
  theme(legend.position = "none") +
  labs(
    x = "Human logFC",
    y = "Chimp logFC",
    title = "Shared DEGs: trajectory-specific conservation"
  )

# ----------------------------
df_stats <- df_all %>%
  group_by(trajectory) %>%
  summarise(
    r2 = summary(lm(C ~ H))$r.squared,
    p = summary(lm(C ~ H))$coefficients[2,4],
    .groups = "drop"
  )

# ----------------------------

ggplot(df_all, aes(x = H, y = C)) +
  geom_point(alpha = 0.7, color = "steelblue") +
  geom_smooth(method = "lm", se = FALSE, color = "black") +
  geom_hline(yintercept = 0, linetype = "dashed") +
  geom_vline(xintercept = 0, linetype = "dashed") +
  facet_wrap(~ trajectory, ncol = 2) +
  geom_text(
    data = df_stats,
    aes(
      x = -Inf, y = Inf,
      label = paste0("R² = ", round(r2, 3), "\np = ", signif(p, 2))
    ),
    inherit.aes = FALSE,
    hjust = -0.1,

  ) +

library(stringr)
library(tidyr)
library(ggplot2)

traj <- c(
  "H_Day02","H_Day25","H_Day515","H_Day1530",
  "C_Day02","C_Day25","C_Day515","C_Day1530"
)

# Prepare dataframe
df <- TopTable %>%
  filter(Comparisons %in% traj) %>%
  mutate(
    Species = ifelse(str_detect(Comparisons, "^H"), "Human", "Chimp"),
    Stage = str_extract(Comparisons, "Day[0-9]+"),
    DEG = adj.P.Val < 0.05
  )

# Wide format: one row per Gene + Stage
df_wide <- df %>%
  dplyr::select(Gene, Stage, Species, logFC, DEG) %>%
  pivot_wider(
    names_from = Species,
    values_from = c(logFC, DEG)
  ) %>%
  filter(
    !is.na(logFC_Human),
    !is.na(logFC_Chimp)
  )

# Keep genes DEG in ONLY one species
# (Human XOR Chimp)
plot_df <- df_wide %>%
  filter(DEG_Human != DEG_Chimp) %>%
  mutate(
    logFC_Human = abs(logFC_Human),
    logFC_Chimp = abs(logFC_Chimp)
  ) %>%
  dplyr::select(
    Gene,
    Stage,
    logFC_Human,
    logFC_Chimp
  ) %>%
  pivot_longer(
    cols = c(logFC_Human, logFC_Chimp),
    names_to = "Species",
    values_to = "abs_logFC"
  ) %>%
  mutate(
    Species = recode(
      Species,
      "logFC_Human" = "Human",
      "logFC_Chimp" = "Chimp"
    ),
    Stage = factor(
      Stage,
      levels = c(
        "Day02",
        "Day25",
        "Day515",
        "Day1530"
      ),
      labels = c(
        "Day0-Day2",
        "Day2-Day5",
        "Day5-Day15",
        "Day15-Day30"
      )
    )
  )

# Plot
ggplot(plot_df,
       aes(x = Species,
           y = abs_logFC,
           fill = Species)) +

  geom_boxplot(width = 0.7) +

  facet_wrap(~Stage, nrow = 1) +

  scale_fill_manual(values = c(
    "Human" = "black",
    "Chimp" = "white"
  )) +

  scale_y_continuous(limits = c(0, 2)) +

  theme_bw() +

  theme(
    legend.position = "none",
    strip.background = element_blank(),
    strip.text = element_text(size = 12)
  ) +

  labs(
    x = "",
    y = "|logFC|",
    title = "Effect sizes for species-specific DEGs"
  )

library(stringr)

# ----------------------------
# 1. Define trajectories
# ----------------------------
traj <- c(
  "H_Day02","H_Day25","H_Day515","H_Day1530",
  "C_Day02","C_Day25","C_Day515","C_Day1530"
)

# ----------------------------
# 2. Prepare long data
# ----------------------------
df <- TopTable %>%
  filter(Comparisons %in% traj) %>%
  mutate(
    Species = ifelse(str_detect(Comparisons, "^H"), "Human", "Chimp"),
    trajectory = str_extract(Comparisons, "Day[0-9]+"),
    DEG = adj.P.Val < 0.05
  )

# ----------------------------
# 3. Pivot to paired H vs C
# ----------------------------
df_wide <- df %>%
  dplyr::select(Gene, Species, trajectory, logFC, DEG) %>%
  pivot_wider(
    names_from = Species,
    values_from = c(logFC, DEG)
  ) %>%
  filter(
    !is.na(logFC_Human),
    !is.na(logFC_Chimp)
  )

# ----------------------------
# 4. KEEP ONLY species-specific DEGs
#    (DEG in Human XOR Chimp)
# ----------------------------
df_all <- df_wide %>%
  filter(DEG_Human != DEG_Chimp)

# ----------------------------
# 5. Format for plotting
# ----------------------------
df_all <- df_all %>%
  mutate(
    H = logFC_Human,
    C = logFC_Chimp,
    trajectory = factor(
      trajectory,
      levels = c(
        "Day02",
        "Day25",
        "Day515",
        "Day1530"
      ),
      labels = c(
        "Day0-Day2",
        "Day2-Day5",
        "Day5-Day15",
        "Day15-Day30"
      )
    )
  )

# ----------------------------
# 6. Scatter plots + regression
# ----------------------------
ggplot(df_all,
       aes(x = H,
           y = C,
           color = trajectory)) +

  geom_point(alpha = 0.7) +

  geom_smooth(
    method = "lm",
    se = FALSE,
    fullrange = TRUE
  ) +

  geom_hline(
    yintercept = 0,
    linetype = "dashed"
  ) +

  geom_vline(
    xintercept = 0,
    linetype = "dashed"
  ) +

  facet_wrap(~ trajectory, ncol = 2) +

  theme_bw() +

  theme(
    legend.position = "none"
  ) +

  labs(
    x = "Human logFC",
    y = "Chimp logFC",
    title = "Species-specific DEGs: trajectory divergence"
  )

# ----------------------------
# 7. R² per trajectory
# ----------------------------
df_stats <- df_all %>%
  group_by(trajectory) %>%
  summarise(
    r2 = summary(lm(C ~ H))$r.squared,
    p = summary(lm(C ~ H))$coefficients[2,4],
    .groups = "drop"
  )

# ----------------------------
# 8. Scatter + R² labels
# ----------------------------
ggplot(df_all,

library(dplyr)
library(tidyr)
library(stringr)
library(ggplot2)

# Comparisons to include
traj <- c(
  "H_Day02","H_Day25","H_Day515","H_Day1530",
  "C_Day02","C_Day25","C_Day515","C_Day1530"
)

# Prepare dataframe
df <- TopTable %>%
  filter(Comparisons %in% traj) %>%
  mutate(
    Species = ifelse(str_detect(Comparisons, "^H"), "Human", "Chimp"),
    trajectory = str_extract(Comparisons, "Day[0-9]+"),
    DEG = adj.P.Val < 0.05
  )

# Wide format
df_all <- df %>%
  dplyr::select(Gene, Species, trajectory, logFC, DEG) %>%
  pivot_wider(
    names_from = Species,
    values_from = c(logFC, DEG)
  )

# Remove missing values
df_all <- df_all %>%
  filter(
    !is.na(logFC_Human),
    !is.na(logFC_Chimp),
    !is.na(DEG_Human),
    !is.na(DEG_Chimp)
  )

# KEEP genes non-significant in BOTH species
df_all <- df_all %>%
  filter(
    DEG_Human == FALSE &
    DEG_Chimp == FALSE
  )

# Rename trajectory labels
df_all <- df_all %>%
  mutate(
    trajectory = recode(
      trajectory,
      "Day02"   = "Day0-Day2",
      "Day25"   = "Day2-Day5",
      "Day515"  = "Day5-Day15",
      "Day1530" = "Day15-Day30"
    )
  )

# Set factor order
df_all$trajectory <- factor(
  df_all$trajectory,
  levels = c(
    "Day0-Day2",
    "Day2-Day5",
    "Day5-Day15",
    "Day15-Day30"
  )
)

# Create plotting variables
df_all <- df_all %>%
  mutate(
    H = logFC_Human,
    C = logFC_Chimp
  )

# Calculate statistics
df_stats <- df_all %>%
  group_by(trajectory) %>%
  do({
    fit <- lm(C ~ H, data = .)

    data.frame(
      r2 = round(summary(fit)$r.squared, 3),
      p = format(
        summary(fit)$coefficients[2, "Pr(>|t|)"],
        scientific = TRUE,
        digits = 2
      )
    )
  })

# Plot
ggplot(df_all, aes(x = H, y = C)) +

  geom_point(
    alpha = 0.5,
    color = "grey40"
  ) +

  geom_smooth(
    method = "lm",
    se = FALSE,
    color = "black"
  ) +

  geom_hline(
    yintercept = 0,
    linetype = "dashed"
  ) +

  geom_vline(
    xintercept = 0,
    linetype = "dashed"
  ) +

  facet_wrap(
    ~ trajectory,
    ncol = 2
  ) +

  geom_text(
    data = df_stats,
    aes(
      x = -Inf,
      y = Inf,
      label = paste0(
        "R² = ", r2,
        "\np = ", p
      )
    ),
    hjust = -0.1,
    vjust = 1.1,
    inherit.aes = FALSE
  ) +

  coord_cartesian(
    xlim = c(-15, 15),
    ylim = c(-15, 15)
  ) +

  theme_bw() +

  theme(
    legend.position = "none"
  ) +

  labs(
    x = "Human logFC",
    y = "Chimp logFC",
    title = "Non-DEGs in both species"
  )

  dplyr::select(Gene, Comparisons, logFC) %>%
  
  mutate(
    species = ifelse(str_starts(Comparisons, "H_"), "H", "C"),
    trajectory = str_remove(Comparisons, "^[HC]_")
  ) %>%
  
  group_by(Gene, species, trajectory) %>%
  summarize(logFC = mean(logFC), .groups = "drop") %>%
  
  pivot_wider(names_from = species, values_from = logFC) %>%
  
  filter(!is.na(H), !is.na(C))

library(dplyr)
library(purrr)
library(stringr)
library(tidyr)
library(ggplot2)

days <- c("02", "25", "515", "1530")

prop_df <- map_dfr(days, function(day) {

  x <- RNA_sets[[paste0("Sig_Sp_inter_Traj", day)]]

  tibble(
    trajectory = day,

    INTER_DEG = length(x$DEGs$Gene),
    INTER_NonDEG = length(x$NonDEGs$Gene)
  )
})

# IMPORTANT: use TRUE universe (same logic as trajectory plot)
total_genes <- prop_df$INTER_DEG + prop_df$INTER_NonDEG

prop_df <- prop_df %>%
  mutate(
    INTER_DEG = INTER_DEG / total_genes,
    INTER_NonDEG = INTER_NonDEG / total_genes
  )

prop_long <- prop_df %>%
  pivot_longer(
    cols = -trajectory,
    names_to = "type",
    values_to = "prop"
  )

prop_long$trajectory <- factor(
  prop_long$trajectory,
  levels = c("02", "25", "515", "1530"),
  labels = c("0–2", "2–5", "5–15", "15–30")
)

ggplot(prop_long, aes(x = trajectory, y = prop, fill = type)) +
  geom_col() +
  theme_bw() +
  labs(
    x = "Time window",
    y = "Proportion of genes",
    fill = ""
  )

TopTable <- TopTable_Filt_logcpm_G1_SpTp_RNA_fc_NoRep_No4
ComparisonNames <- ComparisonNames_Filt_logcpm_G1_SpTp_RNA_fc_NoRep_No4
RNA_sets <- RNA_sets_Filt_logcpm_G1_SpTp_RNA_fc_NoRep_No4
fit2 <- fit2_Filt_logcpm_G1_SpTp_RNA_fc_NoRep_No4

traj_info <- list(
  InterTraj02 = list(coef = "Sig_Sp_inter_Traj02", comp = "Day02"),
  InterTraj25 = list(coef = "Sig_Sp_inter_Traj25", comp = "Day25"),
  InterTraj515 = list(coef = "Sig_Sp_inter_Traj515", comp = "Day515"),
  InterTraj1530 = list(coef = "Sig_Sp_inter_Traj1530", comp = "Day1530")
)

cluster_lists <- list(
  InterTraj02  = Inter_02_genes,
  InterTraj25  = Inter_25_genes,
  InterTraj515 = Inter_515_genes,
  InterTraj1530 = Inter_1530_genes
)

direction_results <- setNames(
  lapply(names(traj_info), function(name) {

    info <- traj_info[[name]]

    get_fc_directions(
      traj_label = name,
      coef_name = info$coef,
      comparison_label = info$comp,
      top_table_all = TopTable,
      fit_obj = fit2,
      gene_set = cluster_lists[[name]]
    )

  }),
  names(traj_info)
)

saveRDS(direction_results, "data/DGE/Interaction_Directions_Filt_logcpm_G1_SpTp_RNA_fc_NoRep_No4.RDS")

library(dplyr)
library(purrr)
library(tidyr)
library(ggplot2)

days <- c("02", "25", "515", "1530")

prop_df <- map_dfr(days, function(day) {

  x <- RNA_sets[[paste0("InterTraj", day)]]

  same_n <- length(x$Same_direction$Gene)
  opp_n  <- length(x$Opposite_direction$Gene)

  tibble(
    trajectory = day,
    Same_direction = same_n,
    Opposite_direction = opp_n
  )
})

prop_long <- prop_df %>%
  pivot_longer(
    cols = -trajectory,
    names_to = "type",
    values_to = "count"
  ) %>%
  group_by(trajectory) %>%
  mutate(prop = count / sum(count)) %>%
  ungroup()

prop_long$trajectory <- factor(
  prop_long$trajectory,
  levels = c("02", "25", "515", "1530"),
  labels = c("0–2", "2–5", "5–15", "15–30")
)

ggplot(prop_long, aes(x = trajectory, y = prop, fill = type)) +
  geom_col() +
  theme_bw() +
  scale_fill_manual(
  values = c(
    "Same_direction" = "#2c7bb6",
    "Opposite_direction" = "#d7191c"
  )
) +
  labs(
    x = "Time window",
    y = "Proportion of interaction DEGs",
    fill = ""
  )

library(dplyr)
library(purrr)
library(tidyr)
library(ggplot2)

days <- c("02", "25", "515", "1530")

prop_df <- map_dfr(days, function(day) {

  x <- RNA_sets[[paste0("InterTraj", day)]]

  tibble(
    trajectory = day,

    Same_direction = length(x$Same_direction$Gene),

    Human_higher = length(x$H_pos_C_neg$Gene),
    Chimp_higher = length(x$H_neg_C_pos$Gene)
  )
})

prop_long <- prop_df %>%
  pivot_longer(
    cols = -trajectory,
    names_to = "type",
    values_to = "count"
  ) %>%
  group_by(trajectory) %>%
  mutate(prop = count / sum(count)) %>%
  ungroup()

prop_long$trajectory <- factor(
  prop_long$trajectory,
  levels = c("02", "25", "515", "1530"),
  labels = c("0–2", "2–5", "5–15", "15–30")
)

ggplot(prop_long, aes(x = trajectory, y = prop, fill = type)) +
  geom_col(color = "black", linewidth = 0.3) +
  theme_bw() +
  labs(
    x = "Time window",
    y = "Proportion of interaction DEGs",
    fill = ""
  ) +
  scale_fill_manual(
    values = c(
      "Same_direction" = "grey70",
      "Human_higher"   = "black",
      "Chimp_higher"   = "white"
    )
  ) +
  theme(
    panel.grid = element_blank()
  )

library(dplyr)
library(ggplot2)

# Add labels
r2_df$Group <- "All Expressed"
r3_df$Group <- "All DEGs"
r4_df$Group <- "Shared DEGs"
r5_df$Group <- "Species-Specific DEGs"
r6_df$Group <- "Non-DEGs"

# Combine
all_df <- bind_rows(r2_df, r3_df, r4_df, r5_df,r6_df)

# Factor order
all_df$Transition <- factor(
  all_df$Transition,
  levels = c("Day0-2","Day2-5","Day5-15","Day15-30")
)

p <- ggplot(
  all_df,
  aes(
    x = Transition,
    y = R2,
    group = Group,
    linetype = Group
  )
) +

  # Background highlight
  annotate(
    "rect",
    xmin = 1.5, xmax = 3.5,
    ymin = -Inf, ymax = Inf,
    alpha = 0.1,
    fill = "grey70"
  ) +

  geom_line(
    aes(linewidth = Group),
    color = "black"
  ) +

  geom_point(
    size = 3,
    color = "black"
  ) +

  geom_text(
    aes(label = round(R2, 2)),
    vjust = -1,
    size = 3,
    show.legend = FALSE
  ) +

  scale_linetype_manual(
    values = c(
      "All Expressed" = "solid",
      "All DEGs" = "dashed",
      "Shared DEGs" = "dotted",
      "Species-Specific DEGs" = "dotdash",
      "Non-DEGs" = "twodash"
    )
  ) +

  scale_linewidth_manual(
    values = c(
      "All Expressed" = 1.8,  # bold
      "All DEGs" = 1.2,
      "Shared DEGs" = 1.2,
      "Species-Specific DEGs" = 1.2,
      "Non-DEGs" = 1.2
    )
  ) +

  labs(
    title = "Inter-species correlation peaks at mid-development",
    x = "Differentiation Transition",
    y = expression(R^2),
    linetype = "Dataset",
    linewidth = "Dataset"
  ) +

  ylim(0, 1) +

  theme_minimal(base_size = 14) +
  theme(
    panel.grid.minor = element_blank(),
    panel.grid.major.x = element_blank(),
    axis.text.x = element_text(angle = 0, hjust = 0.5),
    plot.title = element_text(face = "bold")
  )

p
